I usually blot it on, lightly over my whole face and then again a little heavier on my blemishes. It does go on grey. Let it sit for a few minutes. It will mattify and blend to your skin tone. I wouldn't recommend this for anyone with really dark skin, but I think even tan tones can use this. I don't have to blend much near my neck.. it just looks natural on its own. Occassionally I wear Laura Mercier's Secret Camouflage concealer over the BB cream. I also always finish with a Nars powder. Without a finishing powder, the product can look too dewey. Nars \\"beach\\", \\"desert\\", and \\"mountain\\" colored powders all look natural with this BB cream.<br /><br />PROS OF PRODUCT: I waited a whole month before writing this review so that I could comment on how my skin reacts to it over time. I have NEVER before had a product actually make my skin tone look more even. I still have breakouts, but fewer and I seem to get them from products I put on my skin at night and never seem to get new blemishes while I'm actually wearing the bb cream. My skin used to get oily an hour after applying makeup. I would apply powder once I got to school/work and then about every two hours. By the end of the day I could cake on powder and it'd still be oily. With Skin79's Super+ hot pink bb cream, I literally go a whole day without applying additional powder. Part way through the day I might blot my skin with tissue. This is a miracle to me.<br /><br />CONS: BEWARE OF FAKES!! I have watched a ton of videos and read articles on how to tell what is fake.
